                <div class="aws-comp section"> 
                 <div class="content-expander offset-nopad expander-menu-nav-thin expander-menu-left clearfix" id="aws-element-4d8d5335-26ce-4121-8943-55b14dd50ea4" data-expander-name="solutions"> 
                  <div class="content-expander-menu expander-menu-25 expander-menu-content-center expander-menu-copy-right"> 
                   <div class="expander-menu"> 
                    <ul>

                  <div class="content-expander-content expander-content-padding-midpad"> 
                   <ul class="content-wrapper"> 
                    <li id="aws-element-4d8d5335-26ce-4121-8943-55b14dd50ea4-1" class="content-item active"> <h4 class="tab-title" data-target="#aws-element-4d8d5335-26ce-4121-8943-55b14dd50ea4-1" data-toggle="tab">Web 应用程序 <i class="icon-arrow"></i></h4> 
                     <div class="content-item-wrapper"> 
                      <div class="par parsys"> 
                       <div class="aws-comp section"> 
                        <figure class="image-box "> 
                         <a href="/cn/websites/?hp=tile"> 
                          <div class="image parbase"> 
                           <img alt="solutions-slides-webapplications" title="solutions-slides-webapplications" src="//d0.awsstatic.com/Test%20Images/Kate%20Test%20Images/solutions-slides-webapplications.png" /> 
                          </div> </a> 
                        </figure> 
                       </div> 
                       <div class="lead-copy section"> 
                        <div class="lead   "> 
                         <p>使用一组专为现代 Web 应用程序设计的广泛服务构建可扩展的高性能网站。<a adhocenable="false" href="/cn/websites/?hp=tile">了解更多 &raquo;</a></p> 
                        </div> 
                       </div> 
                       <div class="lead-copy section"> 
                        <div class="lead   "> 
                         <p><b>在 AWS 上运行 Web 应用程序的客户<br /> </b></p> 
                        </div> 
                       </div> 
                       <div class="columnbuilder parbase section"> 
                        <div class="row column-builder offset-nopad"> 
                         <div class="three columns "> 
                          <div class="parsys col1"> 
                           <div class="aws-comp section">
